9 package org.locationtech.geomesa.metrics.micrometer
10 
11 import com.typesafe.config.{Config, ConfigFactory, ConfigRenderOptions}
12 import com.typesafe.scalalogging.StrictLogging
13 import io.micrometer.core.instrument.binder.jvm.{ClassLoaderMetrics, JvmGcMetrics, JvmMemoryMetrics, JvmThreadMetrics}
14 import io.micrometer.core.instrument.binder.system.ProcessorMetrics
15 import io.micrometer.core.instrument.{MeterRegistry, Metrics, Tag}
16 import org.locationtech.geomesa.metrics.micrometer.cloudwatch.CloudwatchFactory
17 import org.locationtech.geomesa.metrics.micrometer.prometheus.PrometheusFactory
18 import pureconfig.{ConfigReader, ConfigSource}
19 
20 import java.util.Locale
21 
22 object MicrometerSetup extends StrictLogging {
23 
24   import pureconfig.generic.semiauto._
25 
26   import scala.collection.JavaConverters._
27 
28   private val registries = scala.collection.mutable.Map.empty[String, String]
29   private val bindings = scala.collection.mutable.Set.empty[String]
30 
31   val ConfigPath = "geomesa.metrics"
32 
33   /**
34    * Add registries to the global registry list, based on the default configuration paths
35    *
36    * @param conf conf
37    */
38   // noinspection ScalaUnusedSymbol
39   def configure(conf: Config = ConfigFactory.load()): Unit = synchronized {
40     if (conf.hasPath(ConfigPath)) {
41       implicit val r0: ConfigReader[Instrumentation] = deriveReader[Instrumentation]
42       implicit val r1: ConfigReader[JvmInstrumentations] = deriveReader[JvmInstrumentations]
43       implicit val r2: ConfigReader[MetricsConfig] = deriveReader[MetricsConfig]
44       implicit val r3: ConfigReader[RegistryConfig] = deriveReader[RegistryConfig]
45       val metricsConfig = ConfigSource.fromConfig(conf.getConfig(ConfigPath)).loadOrThrow[MetricsConfig]
46       metricsConfig.registries.foreach { registryConfig =>
47         val config = ConfigSource.fromConfig(registryConfig).loadOrThrow[RegistryConfig]
48         if (config.enabled) {
49           val configString = registryConfig.root().render(ConfigRenderOptions.concise())
50           if (registries.contains(config.`type`)) {
51             val existing = registries(config.`type`)
52             if (existing != configString) {
53               throw new IllegalArgumentException(
54                 s"Registry type ${config.`type`} already registered with a different configuration:" +
55                   s"\n  existing: $existing\n    update: $configString")
56             }
57           } else {
58             val registry = createRegistry(registryConfig)
59             sys.addShutdownHook(registry.close())
60             Metrics.addRegistry(registry)
61             registries.put(config.`type`, configString)
62           }
63         }
64       }
65 
66       if (metricsConfig.instrumentations.classloader.enabled && bindings.add("classloader")) {
67         logger.debug("Enabling JVM classloader metrics")
68         val tags = metricsConfig.instrumentations.classloader.tags.map { case (k, v) => Tag.of(k, v) }
69         new ClassLoaderMetrics(tags.asJava).bindTo(Metrics.globalRegistry)
70       }
71       if (metricsConfig.instrumentations.memory.enabled && bindings.add("memory")) {
72         logger.debug("Enabling JVM memory metrics")
73         val tags = metricsConfig.instrumentations.memory.tags.map { case (k, v) => Tag.of(k, v) }
74         new JvmMemoryMetrics(tags.asJava).bindTo(Metrics.globalRegistry)
75       }
76       if (metricsConfig.instrumentations.gc.enabled && bindings.add("gc")) {
77         logger.debug("Enabling JVM garbage collection metrics")
78         val tags = metricsConfig.instrumentations.gc.tags.map { case (k, v) => Tag.of(k, v) }
79         new JvmGcMetrics(tags.asJava).bindTo(Metrics.globalRegistry)
80       }
81       if (metricsConfig.instrumentations.processor.enabled && bindings.add("processor")) {
82         logger.debug("Enabling JVM processor metrics")
83         val tags = metricsConfig.instrumentations.processor.tags.map { case (k, v) => Tag.of(k, v) }
84         new ProcessorMetrics(tags.asJava).bindTo(Metrics.globalRegistry)
85       }
86       if (metricsConfig.instrumentations.threads.enabled && bindings.add("threads")) {
87         logger.debug("Enabling JVM thread metrics")
88         val tags = metricsConfig.instrumentations.threads.tags.map { case (k, v) => Tag.of(k, v) }
89         new JvmThreadMetrics(tags.asJava).bindTo(Metrics.globalRegistry)
90       }
91     }
92   }
93 
94   /**
95    * Create a new registry
96    *
97    * @param conf configuration for the registry
98    * @return
99    */
100   def createRegistry(conf: Config): MeterRegistry = {
101     implicit val reader: ConfigReader[RegistryConfig] = deriveReader[RegistryConfig]
102     val config = ConfigSource.fromConfig(conf).loadOrThrow[RegistryConfig]
103     config.`type`.toLowerCase(Locale.US) match {
104       case "prometheus" => logger.debug("Creating prometheus registry"); PrometheusFactory(conf)
105       case "cloudwatch" => logger.debug("Creating cloudwatch registry"); CloudwatchFactory(conf)
106       case t => throw new IllegalArgumentException(s"No registry type defined for '$t' - valid values are: prometheus, cloudwatch")
107     }
108   }
109 
110   private case class MetricsConfig(
111       registries: Seq[Config],
112       instrumentations: JvmInstrumentations,
113     )
114 
115   private case class Instrumentation(enabled: Boolean = false, tags: Map[String, String] = Map.empty)
116 
117   private case class JvmInstrumentations(
118       classloader: Instrumentation = Instrumentation(),
119       memory: Instrumentation = Instrumentation(),
120       gc: Instrumentation = Instrumentation(),
121       processor: Instrumentation = Instrumentation(),
122       threads: Instrumentation = Instrumentation(),
123     )
124 
125   private case class RegistryConfig(
126       `type`: String,
127       enabled: Boolean = true,
128     )
129 }
